8#ifndef APP_MODULE_ACCELTEMP_H_
9#define APP_MODULE_ACCELTEMP_H_
10
11// Accelerometer commands
12#define ACC_ADDR 0x6B << 1 // Use 8-bit address, 6A for external
13
14#define ACCEL_AVERAGE_DEPTH_BITS 0x1F
15#define ACCEL_CALC_TILT_BIT 0x80
16#define ACCEL_BUFFER_LENGTH 20 //Must be less than 256 so cnt doesn't rollover.
17
18#define FUNC_CFG_ACCESS 0x01
19#define PIN_CTRL 0x02
20#define DRDY_PULSED_REG 0x0B
21
22#define INT1_CTRL 0x0D
23#define INT2_CTRL 0x0E
24
25#define CTRL1_XL 0x10
26#define CTRL2_G 0x11
27#define CTRL3_C 0x12
28#define CTRL4_C 0x13
29#define CTRL5_C 0x14
30#define CTRL6_C 0x15
31#define CTRL7_G 0x16
32#define CTRL9_C 0x18
33#define CTRL10_C 0x19
34#define STATUS_REG 0x1E
35
36#define MD1_CFG 0x5E
37
38#define OUT_TEMP_L 0x20
39#define OUTX_L_G 0x22
40#define OUTX_L_A 0x28
41#define WHO_AM_I 0x0F
42
43#define ISPU_CONFIG 0x02
44#define ISPU_STATUS 0x04
45#define ISPU_MEM_SEL 0x08
46#define ISPU_MEM_ADDR1 0x09
47#define ISPU_MEM_ADDR0 0x0A
48#define ISPU_MEM_DATA 0x0B
49#define ISPU_DOUT_00_L 0x10
50
51#define ISPU_INT1_CTRL0 0x50
52#define ISPU_INT2_CTRL0 0x54
53#define ISPU_ALGO0 0x70
54
55#define IMU_ACC_ENABLED 1
56#define IMU_GYRO_ENABLED 1<<1
57#define IMU_ISPU_ENABLED 1<<2
58#define IMU_TEMP_ENABLED 1<<3
59#define IMU_ISPU_RST 1<<5
60#define IMU_RELOAD_ISPU_DATA 1<<6
61#define IMU_RELOAD_ISPU 1<<7
62
63#define NTAN 91
64
65// Temperature sensor commands
66#define TEMP_ADDR 0x48 << 1
67#define T_TEMP_REG 0x00
68#define T_CONF_REG 0x01
69#define T_LOW_REG 0x02
70#define T_HIGH_REG 0x03
71
72#define MAX_TEMPR 500 // 50.0 degC
73#define MIN_TEMPR 100
74
75void sleepAccelerometer( void );
76void initAccelerometer( void );
77void updateAccelerometer( void );
78void sleepTemperature( void );
79void initTemperature ( void );
80void updateTemperature( void );
81void initDiagnostics( void );
82void updateDiagnostics( void );
83void changeModeIMU (UNS8 mode);
